   peṣaṇakaraṇe indrasyaudanarūpasvadravyanāśāpatteḥ tatra kasyānugraha iti	pezaNa-karaNe indrasya-odana-rUpa-sva-dravya-nASa-ApatteH tatra kasya-anugrahaH iti
   saṃdehe mukhyatvenāsaṃjātavirodhitvenādhvarakalpāyāṃ	saMdehe muKya-tvena-asaMjAta-viroDi-tvena-aDvara-kalpAyAm
   mukhyabhūtāgnāvaiṣṇavadharmānugrahasyeva,	muKya-BUta-agnOvEzNava-Darma-anugrahasya-iva,
   indradharmodanānugrahakartavyatāpattyā na sarvapeṣaṇaṃ prāpnoti, ataḥ	indra-Darma-udana-anugraha-kartavya-tA-ApattyA na sarva-pezaNam prApnoti, atas-
   piṣṭakacarugrahaṇe evāvirodhāt? kāṃsyabhojinyāyopapādane pūrvapakṣa iva	pizwaka-caru-grahaNe eva-aviroDAt? kAMsya-Boji-nyAya-upapAdane pUrva-pakzaH iva
   siddhānte 'pi sarvapeṣaṇaṃ saṃbhavatyeveti na kaścana pūrvottarapakṣayoḥ	sidDAnte api sarva-pezaNam saMBavati-eva-iti na kaScana pUrva-uttara-pakzayoH
   prayojanabhedaḥ sidhyeti /	prayojana-BedaH siDyA-iti /
   atastaṇḍulacarugrahaṇapakṣe virodhaprasaktāvapyardhapeṣaṇena	atas-taNxula-caru-grahaNa-pakze viroDa-prasaktO=-api-arDa-pezaNena
   tatparihārasaṃbhavānna tadanurodhenendradevatādravyavighātaḥ kartavya	tad-parihAra-saMBavAt-na tad-anuroDena-indra-devatA-dravya-viGAtaH kartavya
   ityardhameva peṣaṇaṃ pūrvapakṣe prayojanaṃ bhinnaṃ sidhyati /	iti-arDam-eva pezaNam pUrva-pakze prayojanam Binnam siDyati /
   yatra hyamukhyasya sarvathā bādhastatra mukhyasyaivānugrahaḥ //	yatra hi-amuKyasya sarvaTA bADaH-tatra muKyasya-eva-anugrahaH //
   adhvarakalpāgatājyadravyagatamadhyatanasarasvatīyāgīyahavirabhimarśanasy.a	aDvara-kalpa-Agata-Ajya-dravya-gata-maDyatana-sarasvatI-yAgIya-haviH-aBimarSanasy.a
   sakṛddhavirabhimarśanasyaiva śāstrārthatvena vṛdhanvatīmantreṇāpi siddheḥ	sakRt-haviH-aBimarSanasya-eva SAstra-arTa-tvena vRDanvatI-mantreNa-api sidDeH
   tadbādhābhāvāt iha tu mukhyendrānugrahe sarvathā pūṣāṅgapeṣaṇasya	tad-bADa-aBAvAt iha tu muKya-indra-anugrahe sarvaTA pUzA-aFga-pezaNasya
   bādhaprasaṅgādardhapeṣaṇaṃ yuktamityeva prayojanaṃ	bADa-prasaFgAt-arDa-pezaNam yuktam-iti-eva prayojanam
   kāṃsyabhojinyāyopapādanenāśrayaṇīyamiti tadevātra prayojanaṃ vaktumiti //	kAMsya-Boji-nyAya-upapAdanena-ASrayaNIyam-iti tat-eva-atra prayojanam vaktum-iti //
   iti pañcadaśaṃ pauṣṇapeṣaṇasyaikadaivatyatvādhikaraṇam //	iti paQcadaSam pOzNapezaNasya-eka-dEvatya-tva-aDikaraNam //
   iti śrīmatpūrvottaramīmāṃsāpārāvārīṇadhurīṇa	iti SrImat-pUrva-uttara-mImAMsA-pArA-vArINa-DurINa-
   kavimaṇḍana-khaṇḍadevaśiṣya-śaṃbhubhaṭṭaviracitāyāṃ bhāṭṭadīpikāvyākhyāyāṃ	kavi-maNxana-KaNxa-deva-Sizya--SaMBu-Bawwa-viracitAyAm BAwwa-dIpikA-vyAKyAyAm
   prabhāvalyāṃ tṛtīyādhyāyasya tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ //	praBAvalyAm tRtIyA-aDyAyasya tRtIyaH pAdaH //
   atra navītāntaṃ samāptam //	atra navIta-antam samAptam //
